### <a id="Equation preservation">Equation preservation</a>

This is the [Varieties.Preservation][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][]. In this module we show that identities are preserved by closure operators H, S, and P.  This will establish the easy direction of Birkhoff's HSP Theorem.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3188" class="Keyword">private</a> <a id="3196" class="Keyword">variable</a> <a id="3205" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a> <a id="3207" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3207" class="Generalizable">β</a> <a id="3209" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3211" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="4768" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#4768" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="4773" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4775" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#4543" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="4778" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2293" class="Record Operator">≅</a> <a id="4780" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#4485" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
 <a id="4783" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#4768" class="Function">lA≅B</a> <a id="4788" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4790" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3015" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="4798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4799" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2926" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="4805" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4397" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="4811" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4813" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#4499" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

  <a id="5678" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5678" class="Function">σ</a> <a id="5680" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5682" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="5684" href="Algebras.Products.html#1808" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5686" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5354" class="Function">SA</a> <a id="5689" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="5691" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5693" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="5695" href="Algebras.Products.html#1808" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5697" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5309" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="5699" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

  <a id="5947" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5947" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="5949" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5951" href="Algebras.Products.html#1808" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5953" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5309" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="5955" href="Relation.Unary.html#1523" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5957" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4374" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="5959" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5001" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="5963" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5947" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="5965" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5967" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4661" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="5973" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="5976" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5976" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5978" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5980" href="Varieties.Closure.html#9523" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="5987" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5988" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="5990" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#1008" class="Field">snd</a> <a id="5994" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4283" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="5996" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5232" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="6000" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#5976" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="6002" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4283" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="6004" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="6005" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

Above we proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.


<pre class="Agda">

<a id="9037" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="9044" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9044" class="Module">_</a> <a id="9046" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9047" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9047" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="9049" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9051" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="9056" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="9059" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9060" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9060" class="Bound">fe₀</a> <a id="9064" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9066" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#906" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="9073" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9074" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9077" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9047" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9078" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9080" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9047" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9081" class="Symbol">}</a>

   <a id="9504" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9504" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="9509" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9511" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9450" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="9513" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#2513" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="9515" href="Algebras.Basic.html#9813" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="9524" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9447" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9527" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="9532" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9533" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9536" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9047" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9537" class="Symbol">))</a>
   <a id="9543" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9504" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="9548" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9550" href="Subalgebras.Properties.html#5835" class="Function">≤-Lift</a> <a id="9557" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9447" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9559" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9457" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

 <a id="9565" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9267" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="9571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9572" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4076" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a><a id="9576" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9577" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9577" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9578" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9580" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9580" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="9581" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9583" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9583" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9585" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9585" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="9588" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9590" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9592" href="Varieties.Closure.html#6008" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="9598" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9599" href="Varieties.Closure.html#11943" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="9603" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9604" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#7993" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="9609" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9583" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9610" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9613" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9629" class="Function">Goal</a>
  <a id="9620" class="Keyword">where</a>
   <a id="9629" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9629" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="9634" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9636" href="Algebras.Basic.html#9813" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="9645" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9577" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="9647" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9648" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="9653" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9654" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9657" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9047" class="Bound">α</a><a id="9658" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="9661" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2293" class="Record Operator">≅</a> <a id="9663" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9580" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
   <a id="9668" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9629" class="Function">Goal</a> <a id="9673" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9675" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3015" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="9683" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9684" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2926" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="9690" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4397" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="9696" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9698" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#9585" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UniversalAlgebra][] library as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

Before doing so, we need to redefine the class product so that each factor comes with a map from the type `X` of variable symbols into that factor.  We will explain the reason for this below.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="10410" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="class-products-with-maps"></a><a id="10417" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10417" class="Module">class-products-with-maps</a> <a id="10442" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10443" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="10445" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10447" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="10452" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="10455" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10456" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10456" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="10458" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10460" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#787" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="10465" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10466" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="10469" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10470" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10470" class="Bound">fe𝓕α</a> <a id="10475" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10477" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#906" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="10484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10485" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10488" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10489" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10491" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10492" class="Symbol">}</a>
 <a id="10495" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10496" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10496" class="Bound">fe₁</a> <a id="10500" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10502" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#906" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="10509" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10511" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10514" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10515" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10517" href="Agda.Primitive.html#810" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10520" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="10525" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10526" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10529" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10530" class="Symbol">)))</a> <a id="10534" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10535" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="10540" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10541" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10544" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10545" class="Symbol">))}</a>
 <a id="10550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10551" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10551" class="Bound">fe₂</a> <a id="10555" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10557" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#906" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="10564" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10565" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10568" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10572" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10575" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10576" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="10580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10581" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10581" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10583" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10585" href="Relation.Unary.html#1101" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10590" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10591" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10599" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="10601" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10602" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10604" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10607" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10608" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="10612" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.ℑ&#39;"></a><a id="10620" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10620" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="10623" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10625" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#787" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="10630" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10631" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10634" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10635" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="10638" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10620" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="10641" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10643" href="Data.Product.html#916" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="10646" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10646" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10648" href="Data.Product.html#916" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="10650" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10651" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10659" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="10661" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10662" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10664" href="Data.Product.html#916" class="Function">]</a> <a id="10666" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10668" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10646" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10670" href="Relation.Unary.html#1523" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="10672" href="Varieties.Closure.html#3790" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="10673" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10674" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10675" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10677" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="10678" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10680" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="10681" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10683" href="Data.Product.html#1167" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="10685" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10686" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10456" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="10688" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10690" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="10692" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10646" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10694" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="10695" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>

Notice that the second component of this dependent pair type is  `(𝑨 ∈ 𝒦) × (X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣)`. In previous versions of the [UALib][] this second component was simply `𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, until we realized that adding the type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣` is quite useful. Later we will see exactly why, but for now suffice it to say that a map of type `X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣` may be viewed abstractly as an *ambient context*, or more concretely, as an assignment of *values* in `∣ 𝑨 ∣` to *variable symbols* in `X`.  When computing with or reasoning about products, while we don't want to rigidly impose a context in advance, want do want to lay our hands on whatever context is ultimately assumed.  Including the "context map" inside the index type `ℑ` of the product turns out to be a convenient way to achieve this flexibility.


Taking the product over the index type `ℑ` requires a function that maps an index `i : ℑ` to the corresponding algebra.  Each `i : ℑ` is a triple, say, `(𝑨 , p , h)`, where `𝑨 : Algebra α 𝑆`, `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦`, and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, so the function mapping an index to the corresponding algebra is simply the first projection.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.𝔄&#39;"></a><a id="11834" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11834" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a> <a id="11837" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11839" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10620" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="11842" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11844" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="11852" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="11854" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="11857" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11834" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a> <a id="11860" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11862" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="11864" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11865" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11865" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="11867" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11869" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10620" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a><a id="11871" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11873" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11875" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="11877" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11865" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="11879" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4245" class="Function Operator">∣</a>

</pre>

Finally, we define `class-product` which represents the product of all members of 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-product&#39;"></a><a id="11995" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11995" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="12010" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12012" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="12020" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12021" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12024" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12025" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12027" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
 <a id="12030" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11995" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="12045" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12047" href="Algebras.Products.html#1808" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="12049" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11834" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a>

</pre>

If `p : 𝑨 ∈ 𝒦` and `h : X → ∣ 𝑨 ∣`, we view the triple `(𝑨 , p , h) ∈ ℑ` as an index over the class, and so we can think of `𝔄 (𝑨 , p , h)` (which is simply `𝑨`) as the projection of the product `⨅ 𝔄` onto the `(𝑨 , p, h)`-th component.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="12318" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12318" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="12336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12338" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11995" class="Function">class-product&#39;</a> <a id="12353" href="Relation.Unary.html#1523" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12355" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4374" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="12356" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12357" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12360" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12361" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12363" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12366" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12367" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="12369" href="Varieties.Closure.html#3790" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="12371" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12372" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="12375" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12318" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="12393" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12395" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4831" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="12401" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12676" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="12408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12409" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5721" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="12412" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12413" class="Argument">fiu</a> <a id="12417" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12419" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10551" class="Bound">fe₂</a><a id="12422" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="12424" class="Argument">fiw</a> <a id="12428" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12430" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10470" class="Bound">fe𝓕α</a><a id="12434" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12436" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12727" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="12441" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12446" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="12454" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12454" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12457" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12457" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="12461" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12463" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10620" class="Function">ℑ&#39;</a> <a id="12466" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12468" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="12476" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12477" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12480" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12481" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12483" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
  <a id="12487" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12454" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12490" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12490" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12492" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="12495" href="Algebras.Basic.html#9813" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="12504" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12505" href="Algebras.Products.html#5256" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="12507" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12490" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12508" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12510" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12511" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12514" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12515" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12519" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12457" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="12523" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12523" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12525" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12527" href="Algebras.Basic.html#9813" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="12536" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12537" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12454" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12540" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12523" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12541" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12543" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12544" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12547" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12548" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12553" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12553" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="12557" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12559" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12561" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12561" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12563" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12566" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12454" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="12569" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12561" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12570" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12572" href="Relation.Unary.html#1523" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12574" href="Varieties.Closure.html#3790" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="12576" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10581" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="12580" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12553" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="12584" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12584" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12586" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12588" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4076" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="12593" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12594" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#993" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="12598" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4283" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="12600" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12584" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12602" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4283" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="12603" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12605" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4397" class="Function">Lift-≅</a>

  <a id="12615" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12615" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="12621" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12623" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12625" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12625" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12627" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12630" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12457" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="12634" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12625" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12635" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12637" href="Relation.Unary.html#1523" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12639" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4374" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="12641" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12642" href="Varieties.Closure.html#3790" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="12644" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12645" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12649" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12615" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="12655" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12655" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12657" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12659" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4462" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="12665" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12666" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12553" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="12670" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12655" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12671" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12676" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12676" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="12683" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12685" href="Algebras.Products.html#1808" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="12687" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12457" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="12691" href="Relation.Unary.html#1523" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12693" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4374" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="12695" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12696" href="Varieties.Closure.html#3790" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="12698" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="12699" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12703" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12676" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="12710" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12712" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4661" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="12718" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12615" class="Function">psllA</a>

  <a id="12727" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12727" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="12733" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12735" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12737" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12737" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12739" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12741" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12742" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12457" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="12746" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12737" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12747" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12749" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2293" class="Record Operator">≅</a> <a id="12751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12752" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#11834" class="Function">𝔄&#39;</a> <a id="12755" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12737" class="Bound">i</a><a id="12756" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12760" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12727" class="Function">llA≅A</a> <a id="12766" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12766" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="12768" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12770" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#3015" class="Function">≅-trans</a> <a id="12778" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12779" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2926" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="12785" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4397" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="12791" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12793" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2926" class="Function">≅-sym</a> <a id="12799" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4397" class="Function">Lift-≅</a><a id="12805" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>


So, since `PS⊆SP`, we see that that the product of all subalgebras of a class `𝒦` belongs to `SP(𝒦)`.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="class-products-with-maps.class-prod-s-∈-sp"></a><a id="12939" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12939" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="12957" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12959" href="Foundations.Truncation.html#3935" class="Function">hfunext</a> <a id="12967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12968" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12971" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12972" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12975" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="12978" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10443" class="Bound">α</a><a id="12979" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12981" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12983" href="Algebras.Products.html#5403" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="12997" href="Relation.Unary.html#1523" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="12999" href="Varieties.Closure.html#3790" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="13000" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13001" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4374" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="13003" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10581" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="13004" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="13007" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12939" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-sp</a> <a id="13025" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13025" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13029" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13031" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#6310" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="13037" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13038" class="Argument">fovu</a> <a id="13043" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13045" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#10551" class="Bound">fe₂</a><a id="13048" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13050" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13025" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="13054" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#12318" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="h-preserves-identities">H preserves identities</a>

First we prove that the closure operator H is compatible with identities that hold in the given class.

      <a id="13851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13852" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13537" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="13854" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟦</a> <a id="13856" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13514" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13858" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟧</a><a id="13859" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="13861" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="13863" href="Function.Base.html#1031" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="13865" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a><a id="13870" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13872" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">≡⟨</a><a id="13874" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13875" href="Terms.Operations.html#6534" class="Function">comm-hom-term</a> <a id="13889" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13890" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13334" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="13893" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#627" class="Bound">𝓥</a> <a id="13895" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13380" class="Bound">α</a><a id="13896" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13898" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13537" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="13900" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13901" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="13903" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13905" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13547" class="Bound">φh</a><a id="13907" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13909" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13514" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13911" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a><a id="13916" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="13917" href="Overture.Preliminaries.html#4949" class="Function Operator">⁻¹</a> <a id="13920" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">⟩</a>
      <a id="13928" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a><a id="13929" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="13931" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13527" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="13933" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟦</a> <a id="13935" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13514" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13937" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟧</a><a id="13938" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13940" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a><a id="13945" class="Symbol">)</a>   <a id="13949" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">≡⟨</a> <a id="13952" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#1130" class="Function">cong</a> <a id="13957" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="13959" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13960" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13578" class="Function">IH</a> <a id="13963" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a><a id="13968" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13970" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">⟩</a>
      <a id="13978" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a><a id="13979" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="13981" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13527" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="13983" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟦</a> <a id="13985" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13516" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="13987" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟧</a><a id="13988" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13990" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a><a id="13995" class="Symbol">)</a>   <a id="13999" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">≡⟨</a> <a id="14002" href="Terms.Operations.html#6534" class="Function">comm-hom-term</a> <a id="14016" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14017" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13334" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="14020" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#627" class="Bound">𝓥</a> <a id="14022" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13380" class="Bound">α</a><a id="14023" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14025" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13537" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="14027" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14028" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="14030" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14032" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13547" class="Bound">φh</a><a id="14034" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14036" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13516" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="14038" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a> <a id="14044" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">⟩</a>
      <a id="14052" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14053" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13537" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="14055" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟦</a> <a id="14057" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13516" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="14059" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟧</a><a id="14060" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14062" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="14064" href="Function.Base.html#1031" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14066" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a><a id="14071" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14073" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">≡⟨</a> <a id="14076" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13334" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="14079" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13358" class="Bound">𝓧</a> <a id="14081" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13380" class="Bound">α</a> <a id="14083" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14084" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13537" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="14086" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟦</a> <a id="14088" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13516" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="14090" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟧</a><a id="14091" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="14093" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13543" class="Bound">φ</a> <a id="14095" href="Function.Base.html#1031" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="14097" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13620" class="Function">preim</a><a id="14102" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14104" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13559" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="14106" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13670" class="Function">ζ</a> <a id="14108" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2923" class="Function">⟩</a>
      <a id="14116" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14117" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13537" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="14119" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟦</a> <a id="14121" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13516" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="14123" href="Terms.Operations.html#2527" class="Function Operator">⟧</a><a id="14124" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14126" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13559" class="Bound">b</a>          <a id="14137" href="Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#3105" class="Function Operator">∎</a>

</pre>

The converse of the foregoing result is almost too obvious to bother with. Nonetheless, we formalize it for completeness.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="14290" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14290" class="Function">H-id2</a> <a id="14296" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14298" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14300" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14301" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14301" class="Bound">β</a><a id="14302" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14304" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14306" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14307" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14307" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14309" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14309" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="14311" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14313" href="Terms.Basic.html#1853" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="14318" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13349" class="Bound">X</a><a id="14319" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14321" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14323" href="Varieties.Closure.html#3339" class="Datatype">H</a><a id="14324" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14325" class="Argument">β</a> <a id="14327" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14329" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14301" class="Bound">β</a><a id="14330" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14332" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13362" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14334" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="14336" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14307" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14338" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="14340" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14309" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="14342" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14344" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13362" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="14346" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="14348" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14307" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14350" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="14352" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#14309" class="Bound">q</a>

</pre>

Again, the obvious converse is barely worth the bits needed to formalize it.

  <a id="16041" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16041" class="Function">IH</a> <a id="16044" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16046" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="16048" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16048" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="16050" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16052" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16053" href="Algebras.Basic.html#9813" class="Function">Lift-Alg</a> <a id="16062" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16063" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15992" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="16065" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16048" class="Bound">i</a><a id="16066" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16068" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15549" class="Bound">α</a><a id="16069" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16071" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2650" class="Function Operator">⊧</a> <a id="16073" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15976" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16075" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2650" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="16077" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15978" class="Bound">q</a>
  <a id="16081" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16041" class="Function">IH</a> <a id="16084" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16084" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="16086" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16088" href="Varieties.Properties.html#4113" class="Function">⊧-Lift-invar</a> <a id="16101" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15503" class="Bound">wd</a>  <a id="16105" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15976" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16107" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15978" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="16109" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="16111" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15569" class="Function">P-id1</a> <a id="16117" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15976" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16119" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15978" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="16121" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15980" class="Bound">σ</a><a id="16122" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16124" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16125" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15995" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16127" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16084" class="Bound">i</a><a id="16128" class="Symbol">))</a>

 <a id="16133" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15569" class="Function">P-id1</a> <a id="16139" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16139" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16141" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16141" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="16143" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16143" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="16145" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16146" href="Varieties.Closure.html#4831" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a><a id="16151" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16152" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16152" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16153" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16155" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16155" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16156" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16158" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16158" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16160" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16160" class="Bound">y</a><a id="16161" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16163" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16165" href="Varieties.Properties.html#3170" class="Function">⊧-I-invar</a> <a id="16175" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15503" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="16178" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16155" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="16180" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16139" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16182" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16141" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="16184" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16185" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#15569" class="Function">P-id1</a> <a id="16191" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16139" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="16193" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16141" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="16195" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16143" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="16197" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16158" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16198" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16200" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16160" class="Bound">y</a>

</pre>

...and conversely...

<a id="16251" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="16258" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16258" class="Module">_</a>  <a id="16261" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16262" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16262" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="16265" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16267" href="Foundations.Welldefined.html#3233" class="Function">SwellDef</a><a id="16275" class="Symbol">){</a><a id="16277" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16277" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="16279" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16281" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#787" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="16286" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13303" class="Generalizable">𝓧</a><a id="16287" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16289" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16290" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16290" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16292" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16294" href="Relation.Unary.html#1101" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16299" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16300" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16308" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a> <a id="16310" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16311" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16313" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16316" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="16317" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="16320" class="Keyword">where</a>

#### <a id="v-preserves-identities">V preserves identities</a>

Finally, we prove the analogous preservation lemmas for the closure operator `V`.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="16624" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Vid"></a><a id="16631" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16631" class="Module">Vid</a> <a id="16635" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16636" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16636" class="Bound">fe</a> <a id="16639" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16641" href="Foundations.Extensionality.html#2528" class="Function">DFunExt</a><a id="16648" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16650" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16650" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="16653" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16655" href="Foundations.Welldefined.html#3233" class="Function">SwellDef</a><a id="16663" class="Symbol">){</a><a id="16665" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16665" class="Bound">𝓧</a> <a id="16667" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16669" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="16674" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16676" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16677" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16677" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="16679" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16681" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#787" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="16686" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16665" class="Bound">𝓧</a><a id="16687" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16689" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16690" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#16690" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="16692" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16694" href="Relation.Unary.html#1101" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="16699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16700" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="16708" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a> <a id="16710" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="16711" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="16713" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="16716" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="16717" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="16720" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="19561" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#18357" class="Function">V-id1&#39;</a> <a id="19568" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19568" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="19570" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19570" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="19572" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19572" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="19574" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19575" href="Varieties.Closure.html#6008" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a><a id="19580" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19581" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19581" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="19582" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19584" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19584" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="19585" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19587" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19587" class="Bound">VA</a> <a id="19590" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19590" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="19593" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19595" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19597" href="Varieties.Properties.html#3170" class="Function">⊧-I-invar</a> <a id="19607" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#18246" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="19610" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19584" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="19612" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19568" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="19614" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19570" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="19616" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19617" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#18357" class="Function">V-id1&#39;</a> <a id="19624" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19568" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="19626" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19570" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="19628" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19572" class="Bound">σ</a> <a id="19630" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19587" class="Bound">VA</a><a id="19632" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="19633" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#19590" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="class-identities">Class identities</a>

From `V-id1` it follows that if 𝒦 is a class of structures, then the set of identities modeled by all structures in `𝒦` is equivalent to the set of identities modeled by all structures in `V 𝒦`.  In other terms, `Th (V 𝒦)` is precisely the set of identities modeled by `𝒦`.   We formalize this observation as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="20036" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="20043" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20043" class="Module">_</a> <a id="20045" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20046" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20046" class="Bound">fe</a> <a id="20049" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20051" href="Foundations.Extensionality.html#2528" class="Function">DFunExt</a><a id="20058" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20060" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20060" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="20063" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20065" href="Foundations.Welldefined.html#3233" class="Function">SwellDef</a><a id="20073" class="Symbol">){</a><a id="20075" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20075" class="Bound">𝓧</a> <a id="20077" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20079" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="20084" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20086" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20087" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20087" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="20089" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20091" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#787" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="20096" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20075" class="Bound">𝓧</a><a id="20097" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20099" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20100" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20100" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="20102" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20104" href="Relation.Unary.html#1101" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="20109" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20110" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20118" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a> <a id="20120" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20121" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20123" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="20126" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="20127" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="20130" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="20138" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20138" class="Function">ovu</a> <a id="20142" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20142" class="Function">lovu</a> <a id="20147" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20149" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a>

 <a id="20188" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20188" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="20190" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20192" href="Relation.Unary.html#1101" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="20197" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20198" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20206" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20142" class="Function">lovu</a> <a id="20211" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20212" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20214" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20215" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="20220" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20142" class="Function">lovu</a><a id="20224" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="20227" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20188" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="20229" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20231" href="Varieties.Closure.html#5334" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="20232" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20233" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20118" class="Bound">α</a><a id="20234" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20236" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20142" class="Function">lovu</a><a id="20240" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20242" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20100" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="20245" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20245" class="Function">𝒱</a> <a id="20247" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20249" href="Relation.Unary.html#1101" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="20254" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20255" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20263" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20138" class="Function">ovu</a> <a id="20267" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20268" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20270" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20142" class="Function">lovu</a>

</pre>


Once again, and for the last time, completeness dictates that we formalize the coverse of `V-id1`, however obvious it may be.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="20838" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="20845" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20845" class="Module">_</a> <a id="20847" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20848" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20848" class="Bound">wd</a> <a id="20851" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20853" href="Foundations.Welldefined.html#3233" class="Function">SwellDef</a><a id="20861" class="Symbol">){</a><a id="20863" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20863" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="20865" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20867" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#787" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="20872" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#13303" class="Generalizable">𝓧</a><a id="20873" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20875" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20875" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="20877" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20879" href="Relation.Unary.html#1101" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="20884" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20885" href="Algebras.Basic.html#6023" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="20893" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a> <a id="20895" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#611" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="20896" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="20898" href="Algebras.Products.html#3004" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="20901" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3205" class="Generalizable">α</a><a id="20902" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="20905" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="20913" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20913" class="Function">V-id2</a> <a id="20919" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20921" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20922" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20922" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="20924" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20924" class="Bound">q</a> <a id="20926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20928" href="Terms.Basic.html#1853" class="Datatype">Term</a> <a id="20933" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20863" class="Bound">X</a><a id="20934" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20936" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20939" href="Varieties.Closure.html#5334" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="20940" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20941" class="Argument">β</a> <a id="20943" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20945" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#3207" class="Generalizable">β</a><a id="20946" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20948" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20875" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="20950" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="20952" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20922" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="20954" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="20956" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20924" class="Bound">q</a><a id="20957" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20959" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20961" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20962" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20875" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="20964" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">⊫</a> <a id="20966" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20922" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="20968" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html#2728" class="Function Operator">≈</a> <a id="20970" href="Varieties.Preservation.html#20924" class="Bound">q</a><a id="20971" class="Symbol">)</a>
